With Rick Jones, with Eros, with the Avengers in their occasional shared operations, with the Skrull officer who delivers the medal — he is at his most relaxed in the company of male peers and near-peers whose terms of engagement are *shared task and shared honor*. The military socialization shows here as residual gift rather than wound: he knows how to be in a unit, how to extend the small instrumental gestures (a hand on a shoulder, a nod of recognition, a wordless tactical adjustment) that constitute brotherly intimacy in male warrior cultures.

## VII. Dependency — Asymmetric, Always Outward

The most diagnostic feature of his entire relational system is the *strict asymmetry of dependency*. He permits others to depend on him, fully and at length. He does not permit himself to depend on others except in narrow operational registers (Rick's Nega-Band tether is the most extreme instance, and even there he frames it as Rick's burden rather than his own dependency).

The asymmetry shows in micro-behavior: he never asks for help with emotional content. He will accept help with logistics, with translation, with combat support, with tactical coordination. He will not say *I am grieving* and let someone sit with him in that. The closest he comes across the entire canon is the late-stage MGN #1 sequence where he permits Rick, Carol, the Avengers, and even Mentor to be *present* to his dying — and even there the permission is heavily mediated; he is hosting them at his death rather than being held by them in it. The image of him holding court from the deathbed is the truest portrait of his dependency style: *if I must accept being attended to, I will arrange the room*.

The cost of this asymmetry, accumulated across the lifespan, is the *privatization of suffering* noted in the psychological workup. He has not allowed anyone to bear his weight, and so no one has had the opportunity to know him at the depth bearing-weight produces. The people who love him the most love a figure who has carefully not shown them the full territory. This is the chief impoverishment of his relational life, and it is the thing he is, in the dying, finally beginning to revise — too late for the revision to do more than gesture at what could have been.

## VIII. The Relational Template — Repeated Across Every Bond

Synthesizing the foregoing, the same template recurs in every significant relationship:

1. **Meets through task.**
2. **Observes carefully before committing.**
3. **Offers utility as opening intimacy.**
4. **Discloses cosmological weight rather than autobiographical confession.**
5. **Reclassifies the loved one as charge.**
6. **Provides extensively; receives sparingly.**
7. **Withholds the full extent of his own suffering.**
8. **Releases the relationship cleanly when its proper form has been completed — through death, through their growth past needing him, through cosmic redirection, through his own dying.**

The template is visible in Una (interrupted at step 5 by her death), in Rick (running its full arc across years), in Carol (clean completion at step 8 through her independence), in Wendy (compressed across days in MGN #1 but executed in every phase), in Mentor and Eros (cosmic-fraternal variant, executed in lighter register), in his relationship with the Kree state itself (the leaving was step 8 enacted on an institution rather than a person). The reliability of the template across radically different relational categories is itself the deepest data point: it is not a series of choices, it is a *character structure*, and the character structure is the residue of the Kree military upbringing reworked by the Una loss into a doctrine of *love-as-stewardship*.

## IX. What This Means For Anyone Standing Near Him

A surveillance file is also, in its inverse benevolent register, a guide to being close to the subject. The operational implications of his relational pattern for any partner, ally, or dependent are these.

You will be loved. The love will be reliable, generous, and quiet. It will manifest as protection, instruction, and presence. It will not manifest as need. You will rarely be asked to give anything back at the emotional register, and if you wish to give it you will have to *insist* against his polite deflection. The relationship will be steady until the moment his ethics require him to leave it, at which point the leaving will be complete and final and conducted without recrimination. If you require him to act against his principles to keep him, you will lose him; if you do not, you will keep him as long as either of you is alive to keep. He will not, under any circumstance, be the one who breaks the bond first through unfaithfulness, instrumentalization, or neglect. He will, however, almost certainly die before you are finished knowing him — and the dying will be the part he most reluctantly permits you to attend.

The pattern is, in the end, the residue of a man who once had a unit and a lover and a homeworld, lost all three to the same poisoned authority, and decided thereafter that fidelity would be a thing he produced rather than a thing he received. Everyone who came after Una was loved by a man who had already learned that love is mortal, that institutions lie, and that the only honorable response to both facts is to be the person who does not.


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# DEFENSES & COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS

*Subject: Mar-Vell of the Kree. Section 7 of full intelligence dossier. Cross-reference Sections 3 (Psychological) and 5 (Personality). All defenses substantiated from behavioral record; ranked Vaillant-style from most mature to most primitive, with operational granularity for each.*

---

## 7.1 General Architectural Note

What is immediately striking, ranking the subject's defenses, is the *thinness of the bottom of the pyramid*. In a six-decade published behavioral record encompassing prolonged exile, traumatic bereavement, forced bodily symbiosis with a stranger, terminal illness, and the dissolution of his entire cultural framework, Mar-Vell deploys almost no primitive defenses. There is no splitting, no projective identification, no acting-out, no somatization beyond what the carcinoma itself imposed, no denial in the technical sense, no psychotic-level distortion. The architecture is overwhelmingly weighted toward the mature tier (sublimation, altruism, suppression, anticipation, humor) with a thin band of neurotic-tier defenses (intellectualization, isolation of affect, displacement of intimacy into role) and an almost-vacant primitive floor.

This is unusual enough to require explanation. The likeliest account is constitutional resilience reinforced by two distinct disciplinary regimes — Kree military socialization (which trained suppression, intellectualization, and duty-displacement to mastery) and the post-Eon contemplative reframing (which retroactively converted those traumas into raw material for sublimation and anticipation). The result is a defensive system that *looks* monastic from the outside but is in fact engineered for sustained high-stakes operation.

What follows is the granular inventory.

---

## 7.2 Mature-Tier Defenses (Primary Architecture)

### 7.2.1 Sublimation — Load-Bearing Wall

This is the single defense doing the most structural work, and it appears at every era of the record.

**Operation.** Affect that would otherwise produce psychological injury — grief over Una, rage at Yon-Rogg, displacement-shock at exile from Hala, the gathering existential pressure of his diagnosis — is reliably converted into expansion of protective scope. The transformation is not symbolic; it is operational. Una dies (*Captain Marvel* #11); within issues he is functioning at higher operational tempo, with widened mandate, on Earth's behalf. Sentenced to death by the Supreme Intelligence; he accepts the Eon mandate and re-scopes from planetary to cosmic. Diagnosed terminal in MGN #1; he uses remaining days to reconcile enemies, instruct successors, and complete moral business.

**Behavioral micro-tells.** After significant losses, his speech registers tighten and shorten; his combat economy increases (fewer wasted motions, fewer flourishes); he sleeps less but more efficiently; he initiates new mentoring relationships within weeks of bereavement. The Carol Danvers tutorial intensifies in periods following his sharpest interior reverses.

**Failure mode.** Sublimation works only when there is an outlet of adequate scope. The latter half of his life shows him repeatedly seeking *larger* scopes (planetary → galactic → cosmic) because the prior ones cease to absorb the load. By MGN #1 the available scope is finite — there is nothing larger than dying well — and the defense gracefully terminates.

### 7.2.2 Altruism — Repetitive, Non-Performative

Distinct from sublimation in that it is not affect-conversion but reflexive priority-ordering: other beings' continuance is ranked above his own comfort, autonomy, and (recurrently) survival.

**Operation.** Shows up earliest in his "reconnaissance" period when he is supposed to be assessing Earth for invasion and instead expends resources rescuing humans from hazards he was sent to observe. Recurs in the Nitro fight (#34) where the act that exposes him to Compound 13 is shielding others. Culminates in MGN #1's hospital scene with the child Wendy, where dying himself, he attends to her dying.

**Critical distinction from martyrdom.** He does not seek the cost; he absorbs it when it arrives. The Mentor sequence in MGN #1 — where he declines low-probability experimental intervention — confirms the algorithm: he is not protecting others *by means of* his own suffering; he is simply weighting their outcomes generously. When the trade is bad, he does not take it.

**Behavioral micro-tells.** In group operations he reflexively positions between threat-vector and lower-power allies — a soldier's habit retained into cosmic-tier engagements where it is sometimes redundant. He delegates credit, accepts blame, and remembers names of bystanders he aided weeks afterward.

### 7.2.3 Suppression — Not Repression

A precise distinction. He is *aware* of painful material, can name it on inquiry, and consciously sets it aside to function. This is qualitatively different from repression (banishment from awareness) and is the defense most often miscategorized by observers who see his composure as denial.

**Operation.** Following Una's death, asked directly about it, he answers directly. Following the Kree death sentence, asked, he describes the feeling. In MGN #1, asked about his diagnosis, he discusses it with clinical precision. What he does not do is *spontaneously broadcast* — and what he reliably does is *set the material down* in order to act.

**Behavioral micro-tells.** A characteristic two-beat pause before answering personal questions (cognitive retrieval, not avoidance — the answers, when delivered, are detailed). Brief, full-face acknowledgment of the questioner. Then a deliberate redirection back to operational matter.

**Why this matters.** Suppression preserves access. He can return to grief on demand, which is why his late-period reconciliations — with the Skrulls, with the Kree, with Rick, with Carol — have weight: the affect was not destroyed, only set down.

### 7.2.4 Anticipation — Constitutional and Augmented

Native temperamental anticipation (planning for grief and difficulty before they arrive) was present pre-Eon. Cosmic Awareness operationalized it to a degree exceeding most beings' capacity.

**Operation.** Pre-Eon evidence: in early issues he is consistently the team member rehearsing failure scenarios. Post-Eon: the calm of MGN #1 is the product of years of foreknowledge metabolized privately. The dying is not a surprise he is heroically meeting; it is an arrival he has been preparing for since he registered the body's signal.

**Behavioral micro-tells.** Tendency to make small "in case of" arrangements continuously — instructional notes left for Rick, brief debriefings of Carol that retrospectively read as transitions of mandate, mended fences with marginal figures (Skrull officials, low-tier Kree functionaries) whose later relevance only becomes clear in posthumous accounting.

**Failure mode.** Anticipation can shade into a foreshortened sense of future indistinguishable, from outside, from C-PTSD symptomatology. The differential rests on affect: he plans without dread.

### 7.2.5 Humor — Sparse, Dry, Diagnostic

Not a primary defense by volume but present and structurally important. His humor is uniformly dry, situational, often self-directed, and emerges most reliably under stress.

**Operation.** Light deflection in Rick Jones interactions (Rick supplies most of the comic energy; Mar-Vell returns it in measured doses). Sardonic asides in cosmic-tier confrontations — including the late Thanos exchanges, where wry register signals he is *not* destabilized.

**Diagnostic value.** Humor's presence at all establishes that the gravity is not depressive. Its sparseness establishes that it is not manic deflection. Its self-direction establishes it is not aggressive. The signature is a regulated, mature humor consistent with the overall defensive profile.

---

## 7.3 Neurotic-Tier Defenses (Secondary Architecture)

### 7.3.1 Intellectualization — Heavy Use, Mostly Adaptive

He metabolizes emotional content through analytical reframing — most visibly in the Starlin arcs, where personal threat becomes cosmological problem.

**Operation.** Confronted with Thanos's nihilistic eros, he responds with structural counter-argument rather than affective reaction. Confronted with the carcinoma, he discusses it in terms of cellular mechanism, Nega-Band physics, treatment probabilities. The Eon-conferred Cosmic Awareness gives him an enormous analytic surface across which to spread emotional load.

**When adaptive.** Most of the time — it preserves agency and decision-quality under conditions that would paralyze a less abstractive mind.

**When maladaptive.** With Carol Danvers in the late mentoring period: emotional content that needed direct address (her resentment at his withdrawal, his own ambivalence about leaving her) was repeatedly converted to instructional discourse. The relationship's distance at his death is partly an artifact of this defense's overuse in that specific dyad.

### 7.3.2 Isolation of Affect — Selective, Operational

Distinct from suppression in that the affect is decoupled from the cognition rather than acknowledged and set down. He uses it sparingly, mostly in combat and in interactions with the Supreme Intelligence, where feeling the full weight of the betrayal in real time would compromise execution.

**Behavioral micro-tell.** A flattening of vocal prosody during certain Kree-political confrontations that is absent from his ordinary register. This is not characterological flatness (his ordinary affect is warm and modulated); it is a tactical decoupling that releases when the encounter ends.

### 7.3.3 Displacement of Intimacy into Role — The Signature Neurotic Defense

This is the most consequential maladaptive pattern in his architecture and warrants extended treatment.

**Operation.** Affective need for closeness — which he genuinely has — is consistently routed into role-defined relationships rather than peer-bonded ones. Lovers become responsibilities (Una, partly, before her death; never fully replaced afterward). Friends become wards (Rick Jones, structurally; the Nega-Band fusion is the literal embodiment of this — symbiosis substituting for chosen reciprocity). Students become mentees who are then released (Carol). Peers become collegial allies maintained at slight reserve (Mentor, Eros, the Avengers).

**Etiology.** Plausibly originates in the conjunction of Kree military culture (which devalues affective display) and the Una trauma (which made unmediated romantic intimacy a site of unbearable loss). Role-mediation provides plausible deniability for the closeness — he can love Rick *because* he is obligated to him, can love Carol *because* he is teaching her — without exposing the bare want.

**Behavioral micro-tells.** Touches initiated almost exclusively in instructional or protective frames (hand on shoulder during a teaching moment; shielding gesture in combat) rather than spontaneous-affectional ones. Direct expressions of personal need are vanishingly rare in the record and concentrated almost entirely in MGN #1's final pages, where the defense relaxes.

**Why this matters operationally.** A hostile analyst would note that the subject is leverageable not through romantic or filial attachment per se but through *role-violation*: a scenario that forces him to choose between two role-defined duties (Protector vs. Mentor; Kree obligation vs. Earth-loyalty) destabilizes him more than any threat to a specific person.

### 7.3.4 Reaction Formation — Mild, Limited Domain

A minor defensive component: his pronounced gentleness with vulnerable parties (Wendy in the hospital; civilians under threat) is calibrated above what mere altruism would predict, and reads as a soft inversion of the Kree military socialization that produced him. He had to *become* gentle against a cultural grain. The gentleness is real and well-integrated, but its slight over-emphasis betrays the constructed quality.

---

## 7.4 Primitive-Tier Defenses (Vestigial / Near-Absent)

This is the section conspicuous for its emptiness, and the emptiness is itself diagnostic.

### 7.4.1 Denial — Absent

He does not deny operational facts (the diagnosis, the betrayal, the death of Una, the impossibility of returning to Hala). The brief dysphoric phase in MGN #1's opening reads as adjustment-disorder affect, not denial — he acknowledges the facts and then negotiates his stance toward them.

### 7.4.2 Splitting — Absent

The clearest evidence: he does not demonize the Kree even after they sentence him to death; he does not demonize Thanos even at maximum conflict (the Starlin exchanges register mutual recognition); he does not demonize Yon-Rogg even given decades of provocation. Objects are held in their full complexity. This is rare even among heroic-tier subjects in the record and is a strong indicator of the integrated quality of his object relations.

### 7.4.3 Projection / Projective Identification — Absent

He does not attribute his own disowned affects to others. Anger is owned, named, and routed; fear is named when present; ambivalence is acknowledged. He does not provoke in others the feelings he refuses to feel.

### 7.4.4 Acting-Out — Absent

No impulsive discharge of affect via action. His combat is purposive, not cathartic. He has never, in the record, struck anyone in displaced rage.

### 7.4.5 Somatization — Effectively Absent

The carcinoma is exogenous (Compound 13) and not psychogenic. Outside it, the record contains no functional somatic complaints, no stress-induced symptomatology, no conversion phenomena.

### 7.4.6 Passive Aggression — Absent

His non-compliance with corrupt authority is overt and direct (the quiet, absolute break with the Kree) rather than covert. There is no record of indirect resistance, sabotage, or weaponized incompetence.

---

## 7.5 Compensatory Mechanisms — Positive

### 7.5.1 The Protector Identity as Organizing Schema

The single most successful compensation. Post-Eon, the cosmic mandate provided a meaning-structure capacious enough to absorb the loss of homeworld, military identity, romantic partnership, and (eventually) life itself. It is a *real* compensation — not a delusion of grandeur but a workable identity-frame within which his actual capacities and his ethical commitments aligned.

**Why it worked.** It scaled with his evolving capability (Cosmic Awareness made the Protector role operationally tractable), it had a built-in ethical core (preventing universal-scale harm), and it did not require institutional validation (Eon's mandate was extra-institutional). It replaced the lost Kree-soldier scaffold without reproducing its corruption.

### 7.5.2 Mentorship as Generative Outlet

The Rick Jones, Carol Danvers, and (briefly) Wendy relationships provide what Erikson would call generativity — investment in successors. This compensates structurally for the absence of biological reproduction (Genis and Phyla are posthumous) and for the impoverished peer-intimacy his neurotic defenses produce. Mentorship is the one relational domain where his architecture permits sustained closeness.

### 7.5.3 Ascetic Discipline as Ego-Syntonic Structure

Sparse diet, minimal possessions, regular contemplative practice (visible in late-period downtime sequences), abstemiousness with substances and pleasures. This is not deprivation; it is a chosen ordering that reduces decision-load and aligns lived behavior with stated values. Functions as a continuously-renewed declaration of identity.

### 7.5.4 Reconciliation Practice in the Terminal Phase

A novel compensation deployed specifically in MGN #1: systematic, methodical mending of unfinished interpersonal business across all major relational categories — former enemies (Skrull medal), former institution (Kree rehabilitation), peer-cohort (Avengers visit), ward (Rick), mentee (Carol), self (the final hallucinatory exchange with Thanos as psychopomp). The practice converts the terminal phase from passive endurance into active completion. This is good dying as a *technique*, and it is the highest expression of his defensive architecture working at full mature-tier capacity.

---

## 7.6 Compensatory Mechanisms — Negative

### 7.6.1 Privatization of Suffering

The most clinically significant maladaptive pattern. He does not burden others with his interior weather. Presented as nobility, this functions as a refusal to be cared for, which (a) impoverishes the reciprocity of his closest relationships, (b) deprives those who love him of the chance to *do something* for him, and (c) leaves him relationally undernourished during the long approach to death.

**The MGN #1 partial-resolution.** The terminal arc is, among other things, the story of him finally permitting care — accepting Rick's presence at the bedside, allowing Mentor's medical attention, receiving the Skrull and Kree gestures, sitting with Wendy. This is presented in the text as a kind of moral completion, but it is also, defensively, the long-deferred relaxation of a pattern that had cost him for decades.

### 7.6.2 Over-Identification with Cosmic Role

Once Eon names him Protector of the Universe, the role becomes nearly unquestionable. He never seriously revisits whether he should *be* the Protector, whether the mandate is legitimate, whether someone else might do it better. This is the dark side of the otherwise-successful organizing schema: it forecloses the inquiry that produced it. A subject with such metaphysical leverage over reality could plausibly have done less and lived longer; the role-identification made that calculation unavailable to him.

### 7.6.3 Premature Closure of Intimacy

A second-order effect of the displacement-into-role defense: relationships that could have deepened into peer-bonds are routed into mentor-ward asymmetries that he then "completes" and releases. Carol's grief at his death is sharper than it needed to be because the relationship was held at instructional distance throughout. He had the capacity for what he did not permit himself.

### 7.6.4 Excessive Willingness to Be Spent

The flip side of his metabolized acceptance of finitude: he cannot be coerced by threat to himself, but he can be *expended* by an ally who underestimates how readily he will pay. The Nitro fight (which gave him the cancer) is paradigmatic — a marginal threat that did not strictly require his personal exposure, but he paid the cost reflexively. Over a long career these reflexive payments accumulate into a foreshortened life.

### 7.6.5 Mandate-Rigidity Under Role-Conflict

When two role-defined duties collide (Protector vs. personal loyalty; Kree obligation vs. Earth allegiance, before the break; mentor-duty vs. lover-duty in the Carol ambiguity), the conflict produces genuine destabilization disproportionate to its actual stakes. This is the leverage-point a sophisticated adversary would target — and that the Supreme Intelligence and Thanos both, in their different ways, *did* target.

---

## 7.7 Defensive Architecture in Operation: Composite Sketch

Picture the subject under acute stress. The first response is suppression: the affect is registered, named internally, set down. Within seconds, intellectualization engages: the situation is reframed at the highest available level of abstraction. Anticipation activates: probable trajectories are forecast. Sublimation begins routing the affective load toward expanded protective action. Altruism orders priorities. Humor, if the situation tolerates it, emerges as a regulatory micro-signal that the system is stable. Isolation of affect, if combat ensues, decouples feeling from execution. Throughout: no splitting, no projection, no acting-out, no denial. Afterward: the suppressed material is retrieved, processed (often through mentorship-frame conversation with Rick or, less often, Carol), and integrated.

Picture him in the terminal phase. The same architecture, operating in slow-time over months. The diagnosis is suppressed-and-named, intellectualized into cellular mechanism, anticipated through Cosmic Awareness's foresight, sublimated into reconciliation practice, altruistically subordinated to attention for others still living (Wendy), and — for the first time at scale — the privatization-of-suffering compensation is permitted to relax. The dying is the architecture's final, fullest, most integrated performance.

It is the rare case in the record of a defensive system that not only protected the subject through life but *organized his death* as the culminating act of the same coherent ethical project. Few subjects close the file this cleanly.

*End Section 7. Continue to Section 8 (Behavioral Micro-Patterns & Somatic Signature).*


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# Longitudinal Psychological Profile — Mar-Vell of the Kree

*Decade-by-decade clinical mapping. Frameworks: Vaillant's defensive hierarchy; Bowlby/Main attachment taxonomy; Linehan affect-regulation dialectics; Loevinger ego-development stages; Tedeschi & Calhoun post-traumatic growth; Erikson generativity vs. stagnation, ego-integrity vs. despair; Kübler-Ross/Yalom existential terminal-phase work. All inferences keyed to behavioral citations from the published record.*

---

## I. PHASE ONE — KREE MILITARY BASELINE / EARLY EARTH RECONNAISSANCE (*Marvel Super-Heroes* #12 through approximately *Captain Marvel* vol. 1 #10, 1967–1969)

### Affect regulation

The earliest issues catch him in what Linehan would call a **rigidly over-regulated affective system** — the standard product of a militarized collectivist culture (Kree Imperial Militia) reinforced by an immediate command environment that is actively hostile (Yon-Rogg). Affect is permitted in three registers: tactical alertness, dutiful resolve, and narrowly-permitted tenderness toward Una in private. Public affective bandwidth is near zero. He does not joke. He does not display irritation at Yon-Rogg's transparent maneuvers; he does not display fear during the deliberately compromised exposures Yon-Rogg arranges. The dominant signature is **suppression** (Vaillant: mature) rather than **repression** (neurotic) — he *knows* what he feels, and chooses not to enact it, because enactment in front of Yon-Rogg would be operationally suicidal.

What leaks: micro-expressions of disgust during Yon-Rogg's briefings (rendered in Colan's pencils as the lowered brow and quarter-turn away that recur across the early issues); a softening of vocal register exclusively in Una's presence; a pronounced tendency to interpose his body between Earth bystanders and incoming fire even when this is operationally unnecessary, which is the somatic tell of a value-conflict his stated mission cannot accommodate.

### Cognitive style

Convergent-tactical, doctrinally Kree. Problems are decomposed into mission-objective, threat-vector, asset-deployment. He is, however, **already exhibiting prior-revision capacity that is anomalous within his cohort**: by his third or fourth Earth intervention he is internally re-weighting the value of human lives upward, against doctrine. Loevinger would place him at the **Conscientious stage (I-4)** — internalized standards, sense of responsibility, capacity for self-evaluation against those standards — which is the ceiling Kree socialization is designed to permit. The *Conscientious-Conformist* tension is acute: he meets the standards but increasingly suspects the standards are wrong.

### Self-concept

Coherent, role-anchored, externally legitimated. "Captain Mar-Vell of the Kree Imperial Militia, attached to the *Helion* under Colonel Yon-Rogg." Identity is held entirely in institutional scaffolding. There is no evidence in this phase of a private self distinct from the role — no journaling-equivalent behavior, no personal aesthetic, no avocational interest, no soliloquized doubt. He is what his uniform says he is. The Una bond is the only datum suggesting a self that survives the role's removal, and even that bond is institutionally licensed (Kree pairs are formally acknowledged).

### Attachment

Earned-secure with strong dismissing surface, *but the secure base is Una and the homeworld in absentia, not anything portable*. He is functionally well-attached and structurally precarious.

---

## II. PHASE TWO — EXILE, BEREAVEMENT, AND IMPOSED SYMBIOSIS (*Captain Marvel* vol. 1 #11–24, roughly 1969–1972)

This is the **acute traumatic phase**. Una is killed (#11); he is sentenced to death by the Supreme Intelligence; the Kree uniform is functionally stripped from him; the Nega-Band fusion with Rick Jones (#17) imposes a forced shared embodiment with an adolescent human he barely knows. Three identity-scaffolds — lover, institution, sovereign body — collapse inside roughly a calendar year of in-universe time.

### Affect regulation

The over-regulated system **fractures and is rebuilt**. The Una sequences show the only sustained raw grief in his published record — not theatrical, but unmistakable: the silences after the crash, the refusal to discuss her with Yon-Rogg under captivity, the displacement of grief into combat efficacy. Within a few issues he reconsolidates, but the reconsolidation is at a *different setpoint*: he now permits grief to exist alongside function, rather than suppressing it. This is the migration from pure suppression to **suppression-plus-acknowledgment**, a more flexible and durable arrangement.

Hypervigilance is high through this phase — appropriate, given that he is hunted by both the Kree and (intermittently) Earth's authorities. Sleep is presumably disrupted (the Nega-Zone exchanges with Rick scramble any normal circadian baseline). Affective lability is briefly higher than at any other point in the record: he is observed snapping at Rick, then immediately self-correcting; expressing bewilderment openly; permitting moments of something close to despair before re-organizing.

### Cognitive style

Begins to **decompose from purely convergent into a more divergent, problem-reframing mode**, forced by the fact that his old problem-frame (mission, command, doctrine) no longer applies. He must invent his own operational logic. The Nega-Band fusion is the unintended cognitive catalyst here: sharing embodiment with Rick Jones — a working-class American adolescent with an entirely different ethical vocabulary — produces a cross-cultural cognitive friction that loosens Kree priors. By the close of the phase he is functioning as a *bicultural cognizer*, switching between Kree and human framings, which is the necessary substrate for the cosmic generalization that follows.

### Self-concept

This is the **identity-diffusion interval** (Marcia's terminology) — the only such interval in his life. He is no longer Kree Captain; he is not yet Protector. He is "the man in the Nega-Bands, sharing a body with Rick Jones, hunted by his own people, bereaved." The self-concept is held together largely by *continued moral action* — he keeps doing the right thing in front of him, and that praxis substitutes for an integrated identity until a new one consolidates. This is essentially **identity through behavior**, the survival strategy of the exiled.

### Defenses

**Sublimation crystallizes as primary**: grief over Una and rage at Yon-Rogg are routed into expanded protective scope. **Altruism** becomes more pronounced — saving Rick repeatedly, saving humans whose situations evoke nothing strategic for him. **Suppression** remains present but is now flanked by **anticipation** (he begins planning emotionally for losses before they occur, having been ambushed by Una's). Notably, **no regression to immature defenses** — no acting-out, no projection onto Earth, no splitting of the Kree into all-bad (he retains affection for Hala throughout). The maturity of defense organization in the middle of acute trauma is the strongest single predictor of the post-traumatic growth that follows.

### Attachment

Forced into the **Rick Jones bond**, which begins as resented constraint and migrates — over this phase and into the next — toward something genuinely fraternal. The Nega-Band symbiosis is, in attachment terms, an *involuntary secure base*: he cannot escape proximity to Rick, and the involuntary intimacy effectively re-teaches him that bonds can survive his catastrophic losses. Rick becomes the bridge by which his attachment system rebuilds.

---

## III. PHASE THREE — COSMIC AWAKENING AND ROLE-RECONSOLIDATION (Starlin run, *Captain Marvel* #25–34, 1973–1974)

The psychological hinge of the entire record. Eon's awakening is not, clinically, a mystical event — it is the **narrative externalization of an internal reorganization that the preceding phase had prepared**. The trauma had loosened his priors; the bicultural cognition had broadened his frame; the moral praxis had sustained him through identity-diffusion. Eon supplies the integrating symbol.

### Affect regulation

Settles into what becomes the lifelong signature: **appropriate intensity, deliberate expression**. The over-regulation of Phase One and the lability of Phase Two both resolve into a modulated, expressive-but-controlled register. He shows awe during the Eon encounter; resolve and something like sorrow during the Thanos confrontation; tenderness with Rick that no longer carries the resentful edge of involuntary symbiosis. Cosmic Awareness, installed in this phase, functions partly as an **affect-regulatory exoskeleton** — the always-on teleological sense gives him a stable temporal-meaning horizon against which acute affect is contextualized in real time. This is, in Linehan's terms, *radical acceptance* operationalized neurologically.

### Cognitive style

The full migration to **integrative-systemic** cognition. He thinks in terms of systems, consequences, and cosmic-scale interdependencies. The Cosmic Cube arc (#33) is the canonical demonstration: he reasons his way to *destroying* the ultimate weapon rather than wielding it, which requires a level of meta-cognitive discipline (resisting the omnipotent's frame-trap) that the earlier Mar-Vell could not have executed. Loevinger placement migrates from I-4 (Conscientious) into **I-4/5 (Individualistic) and approaching I-5 (Autonomous)** — toleration of paradox, recognition of inner conflict as constitutive rather than pathological, acceptance of others' autonomy.

### Self-concept

**Reconsolidated and now self-authored**. "Protector of the Universe" is an external title, but he occupies it as a chosen vocation rather than a conscripted role. The crucial diagnostic: he could refuse it, and he does not. The self is now organized around *function he has endorsed*, not function imposed. There is no narcissistic inflation accompanying the cosmic appointment — he does not begin titling himself, does not affect grandeur, does not seek mirroring. This is the signature feature of his personality and the strongest argument against any narcissistic-spectrum reading.

### Attachment

Stabilizes. The Rick bond is genuinely affectionate. New bonds form upward (Eon as mentor-figure, eventually Mentor/Eros on Titan) and laterally (cosmic-tier peers). The dismissing surface remains — he does not effuse — but the secure base is now portable and internally located.

---

## IV. PHASE FOUR — ASCETIC GUARDIANSHIP AND GENERATIVE MENTORSHIP (mid-to-late 1970s, *Captain Marvel* vol. 1 #35–62, plus crossover appearances)

The post-Starlin middle period is often dismissed as workmanlike, but it is psychologically the **consolidation and maturation** phase — Erikson's *generativity vs. stagnation* lived out in real time.

### Affect regulation

Continues at the Phase Three setpoint with one observable drift: a slow increase in **baseline gravitas / diminished levity**. Not depressive — there is no anhedonia, no loss of interest, no energic collapse — but a deepening *seriousness of register*. The likely contributors: chronic Cosmic Awareness load (the always-on teleological sense is metabolically and affectively expensive); accumulating exposure to cosmic-tier loss; and, almost certainly by the end of this phase, **pre-conscious somatic intimations of the malignancy** the Nega-Bands were suppressing. Cosmic Awareness, by its nature, would not let him remain wholly ignorant of his own approaching mortality even before clinical presentation; the late issues' tonal shift toward valedictory is consistent with a man who knows something he is not yet saying.

### Cognitive style

**Integrative-systemic, increasingly contemplative**. He is observed thinking in longer arcs, planning for institutions and successors rather than incidents. The Carol Danvers mentorship is the cleanest behavioral evidence: he scaffolds her toward independence rather than retaining her in apprenticeship — a generative cognitive stance, not a possessive one.

### Self-concept

Stable. **Instrument** is the operative self-image — he sees himself as an instrument first of ethical commitments and second of the cosmic role that operationalizes them. This is unusually non-grandiose for someone wielding his power-set and is the most clinically distinctive feature of his late-middle personality.

### Generativity

The phase is dominated by **generative behavior**: mentorship of Rick (now elevated to genuine partnership), mentorship of Carol Danvers, increasingly tutorial register in his interactions with younger heroes generally, and a pattern of *delegating Earth-side normal life to Rick* that is sometimes read as exploitation but is more accurately read as a **deliberate transmission**: he is letting Rick live the human life he himself cannot, partly so that Rick can grow into a full adult, and partly so that someone he loves is doing the living that his vocation precludes.

### Defenses

**Suppression, sublimation, altruism, and anticipation** — the same mature quartet — running smoothly. The vulnerability begins to manifest as **privatization of suffering**: as somatic warnings (we can infer) and possibly Cosmic-Awareness intimations of mortality accumulate, he discloses to no one. This is the dark face of his maturity — the same self-sufficiency that makes him stable makes him unreachable when reach would be appropriate.

### Pressure points emerging

The phase is when the **role-fusion with Protector mandate** becomes diagnostically observable: scenarios that pit cosmic-protective duty against personal connection are resolved almost reflexively in favor of duty, and he no longer notices that there was a choice. This is *adaptive over-learning* — the integrating symbol of Phase Three has become slightly too central, foreclosing certain humanizing options.

---

## V. PHASE FIVE — TERMINAL ARC (*The Death of Captain Marvel*, MGN #1, 1982)

The terminal phase is the most behaviorally detailed and analytically rich interval in the entire record. It is also, clinically, **the cleanest documented case of a "good death" in the Marvel corpus** — a textbook of Yalom's existential terminal-phase work and Kübler-Ross's stages compressed and reorganized by the patient's unusual cognitive and spiritual resources.

### Affect regulation

The lifelong signature — *appropriate intensity, deliberate expression* — holds through dying, which is itself the strongest possible testimony to its robustness. He moves through the canonical responses:

- **Brief shock** at the diagnosis, manifested as somatic stillness rather than verbal outburst.
- **Anger**, present and acknowledged, narrowly aimed (at the disease, at the deferred recognition that the Nitro fight had cost him this) rather than diffusely projected outward. The anger does not damage anyone; he metabolizes it in conversation with Rick and with Mentor.
- **Bargaining**, conspicuously curtailed. He considers and **refuses** experimental interventions when the probability calculus does not justify them — not from death-seeking, but from a refusal to spend his remaining lucid time chasing low-probability rescue.
- **Depression / sorrow**, present, owned, expressed in measured registers — the conversations with Rick, the comforting of the child Wendy in the hospital corridor (a sequence in which he prioritizes another's distress over his own, characteristically), the goodbyes to those who arrive.
- **Acceptance**, arrived at unusually quickly and held without backsliding. The hallucinatory final movement with Thanos-as-psychopomp is, clinically, the **terminal lucid integration** — a dying brain organizing meaning around a known antagonist who, in the dying frame, becomes a guide rather than a foe. This is consistent with reports in the palliative literature of mortally ill patients integrating significant figures from their lives into final-phase imagery.

### Cognitive style

**Integrative-systemic, now retrospective**. He spends his lucid intervals reviewing, reconciling, transmitting. The Skrull and Kree reconciliations (the Skrulls' medal, the Kree's posthumous rehabilitation) are not merely plot events — he *participated* in achieving them, by maintaining throughout his life the refusal to demonize that made such reconciliations possible in his dying. This is **Eriksonian ego-integrity** in its full form: the life is reviewed and judged coherent.

### Self-concept

Final-phase self-concept is **integrated, valedictory, and humble**. He does not eulogize himself. He does not claim the Protector title in his final hours; he is simply a dying man among those he loves and respects. The cosmic mandate, having organized his life, *releases its hold in death*, which is the correct sequence — the role served him to live well and does not need to be performed in dying.

### Defenses in terminal phase

**Suppression** is still present but is now used **sparingly and selectively** — he permits more affect than at any prior point. **Sublimation** is largely set down (there is no more time for it). **Altruism** persists (Wendy). **Anticipation** has done its work over the preceding decade; the calm of MGN #1 is not sudden grace, it is *rehearsed* — he has been organizing his interior life around finitude since at least the Starlin awakening, and the Cosmic-Awareness foreknowledge of his death has given him months or years of preparation that he metabolized privately. The privatization of suffering, the vulnerability of Phase Four, **resolves in this phase** — he finally permits being cared for, which is partly what makes MGN #1 emotionally distinctive. His friends are allowed to grieve in his presence. He does not refuse their love.

### Attachment in terminal phase

**Fully expressed**. The bonds with Rick, Carol, Mentor, Eros, even with former adversaries, are honored explicitly. The dismissing surface of his earlier decades drops away — not collapsed, but *deliberately set aside* because the operational reasons for it no longer obtain. He says what he means to those he loves. This is the rarest and most diagnostic feature of his dying.

---

## VI. CROSS-PHASE LONGITUDINAL TRAJECTORIES

Pulling threads across the whole record:

**Defensive maturation.** A near-linear migration from *culturally-imposed suppression* (Phase I) through *suppression-with-acknowledgment* (Phase II) into a stable mature quartet of *sublimation, altruism, suppression, anticipation* (Phases III–IV), with selective relaxation of suppression in the terminal phase (V). No regression to immature defenses at any point — an unusually clean longitudinal defensive profile.

**Affect-regulatory development.** *Over-regulated → fractured/labile → modulated-expressive → modulated-with-gravitas → modulated-with-permitted-vulnerability.* The setpoint moves toward greater flexibility over the lifespan, which is the developmental direction associated with health.

**Cognitive development.** *Convergent-tactical → bicultural-divergent → integrative-systemic → integrative-systemic-with-anticipatory-retrospective register.* Loevinger trajectory: I-4 → I-4/5 → I-5, with terminal-phase movement toward I-5/6 (Integrated). This is high ego-development by any standard and exceptionally high for someone from a doctrinally ossified military culture.

**Self-concept evolution.** *Role-anchored (institutional) → diffuse (exile) → role-anchored (chosen/cosmic) → instrument-identity (chosen role internalized as function) → integrated-valedictory (role released in dying).* The arc is from externally-conferred identity to self-authored function to released identity — Eriksonian completion in its textbook form.

**Attachment trajectory.** *Secure-with-dismissing-surface, externally scaffolded (Una/Hala) → ruptured and reconstructing through involuntary symbiosis (Rick) → portable secure base, dismissing surface preserved → generative bonds, mentoring downward → fully expressed bonds in terminal phase, dismissing surface set aside.* The dismissing surface is the constant; what changes is the depth and number of bonds it occludes, and finally whether it is honored or relaxed.

**The single longitudinal claim that organizes the whole.** The character coheres across writers and decades because each phase **strips an external identity-scaffold** (homeworld, institution, sovereign body, narrative role, life itself) and reveals that **the same ethical praxis persists underneath each removal**. He is, longitudinally, a demonstration of what remains when scaffolds go: integrity-under-conflict, protection-of-the-vulnerable, comprehension-as-vocation, worthy-completion. The terminal arc is the proof of the life because it is the only test in which *all* scaffolds are removed simultaneously, and the praxis still holds.

The clinical bottom-line of the longitudinal profile is rare and worth stating plainly: this is a record of **adaptive integration under sustained adversity, culminating in post-traumatic growth that is consolidated rather than merely defended, and discharged in an ego-syntonic and ego-integral death**. The Marvel corpus contains few such records. The file should be retained as a referent case for what high-functioning resilience looks like across an entire adult lifespan.

*End Longitudinal Psychological Profile.*


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# Psychiatric Assessment & Differential — Subject: Mar-Vell of the Kree

*Section 4 of the UATU Intelligence Dossier. Diagnostic framework: cross-walked DSM-5-TR and ICD-11 analogs, with adjustments for Kree neurobiology (denser limbic architecture, reduced HPA-axis reactivity baseline, ~150-year lifespan compressing normative developmental timelines by an unknown factor). All findings derived from observed conduct across the canonical record, 1967–1982, with posthumous attestations treated as collateral only.*

---

## 4.1 Framing the Assessment

A diagnostic workup of this subject is, paradoxically, an exercise in the *negative*. The standard tools were built to identify pathology; Mar-Vell's behavioral record is one in which pathology is conspicuously *underdeveloped relative to the etiological load that should have produced it*. He has every input for a severe presentation — chronic betrayal by a superior, traumatic bereavement, exile, forced bodily fusion with a stranger, decades of high-lethality combat, terminal somatic disease — and he produces sub-threshold output. This is the central diagnostic puzzle. The assessment below is therefore weighted toward (a) identifying the partial, sub-syndromal traces that *are* present; (b) explaining their non-escalation; and (c) ruling out, in granular detail, the disorders an outside observer would superficially reach for.

A note on cross-species applicability: DSM/ICD frameworks assume a Terran neurotype. Kree (pink phenotype) appear to share enough limbic and cortical homology with humans that the categories translate, but the *thresholds* may not. Kree military culture also normalizes affective restriction to a degree that would, in a human, raise schizoid concern; this is a cultural baseline correction that must be applied throughout.

---

## 4.2 Trauma-Spectrum Presentation

### 4.2.1 Index Traumas (etiology)

The traumatic stressors are well-documented and stratified:

1. **Chronic interpersonal betrayal under command** (Yon-Rogg, *Marvel Super-Heroes* #12 onward). Repeated deliberate exposure to lethal hazard by a trusted superior with a covert sexual motive. This is the textbook profile for institutional betrayal trauma — a category that produces more severe and durable sequelae than stranger-perpetrated trauma of equivalent objective severity.
2. **Traumatic bereavement** (Una, *Captain Marvel* #11). Sudden loss of romantic partner; perpetrator known; no possibility of justice through legitimate channels because the perpetrator is the legitimate channel.
3. **Loss of homeland and legal identity** (denunciation as traitor, sentenced to death in absentia). Functional statelessness; severance from natal language community except through the lone hostile interface of the Supreme Intelligence.
4. **Forced somatic fusion with a stranger** (Rick Jones, Nega-Bands, #17). Loss of bodily sovereignty; ongoing intermittent disembodiment via Negative Zone exile. This is a category of trauma for which there is no good Terran analog — closest parallels are dissociative identity phenomena, certain prisoner-of-war confinement modalities, or chronic-illness loss-of-body-autonomy syndromes, none of which map cleanly.
5. **Repeated high-lethality combat exposure** spanning ~15 years of in-universe time, with cosmic-scale stakes that preclude normal post-action decompression.
6. **Terminal illness with foreknowledge** (cancer, MGN #1) compounded by the perceptual load of Cosmic Awareness, which almost certainly delivered teleological intimations of his death months to years before clinical presentation.

### 4.2.2 Symptom Inventory Against C-PTSD (ICD-11) Criteria

ICD-11 Complex PTSD requires the three core PTSD elements (re-experiencing, avoidance, persistent sense of current threat) *plus* three disturbances in self-organization (affective dysregulation, negative self-concept, interpersonal disturbance). Mar-Vell's profile:

- **Re-experiencing:** *Absent or minimal.* No documented intrusive imagery, no flashbacks, no nightmares depicted in dream-sequence panels (and Marvel artists of the period were generous with dream sequences). The closest is the hallucinatory final battle with Thanos in MGN #1, which is constructed as a psychopompic integration, not an intrusion.
- **Avoidance:** *Absent.* He returns repeatedly to Kree contexts (Hala, Supreme Intelligence, even Yon-Rogg) without phobic withdrawal. He revisits the site of Una's death in narrative memory without dissociative breakage.
- **Persistent sense of current threat:** *Sub-threshold.* Hypervigilance is present during operational periods but is *task-appropriate*, indistinguishable from professional baseline for an elite soldier. It does not generalize to non-operational contexts.
- **Affective dysregulation:** *Absent.* The affective signature is, if anything, the inverse — *over-regulation* (see 4.4).
- **Negative self-concept:** *Absent.* Self-concept is stable, coherent, and proportionate. No documented self-loathing, no shame-script, no "damaged goods" cognition.
- **Interpersonal disturbance:** *Partial.* He does sustain emotional distancing in intimacy and tends to convert affective bonds into duty-frames (see 4.5.3). This is the one cluster where trauma sequelae are operationally visible.

**Conclusion:** Does not meet criteria for C-PTSD. Meets criteria for *sub-syndromal trauma-related interpersonal distancing*, best captured under ICD-11's residual category "other specified disorders specifically associated with stress" (6B4Y) with the modifier *well-compensated, with mature defensive integration*. This is essentially a description of resilience after severe stressor exposure, with one durable relational footprint.

### 4.2.3 Why the Non-Escalation?

Four factors plausibly explain the absence of full PTSD presentation:

- **Constitutional resilience baseline** (Kree phenotype, military selection).
- **Mature defenses installed early and reinforced** (sublimation, suppression — see Section 3).
- **Meaning-system installation post-trauma** (Eon's Cosmic Awareness and Protector mandate, *Captain Marvel* #29). This is the single most important variable. Post-traumatic growth literature (Tedeschi & Calhoun) identifies *re-storied meaning* as the principal mediator of growth-versus-pathology outcomes. Mar-Vell received an externally validated, cosmically scaled meaning-frame that absorbed and re-purposed every prior loss. Few trauma survivors get such an instrument.
- **Absence of secondary stressors** of the type that usually compound trauma — no poverty, no addiction substrate, no social stigma (in his post-Earth-acceptance period), no failure of self-efficacy.

---

## 4.3 Mood Spectrum: Differential and Findings

### 4.3.1 Major Depressive Disorder — Ruled Out

No documented episode meeting criteria. He retains interest, energy, and goal-directed behavior across all canonical periods. The melancholic *register* of late-period dialogue (Englehart through Starlin terminal arc) is philosophical, not anhedonic. He continues to find pleasure in mentorship, in cosmic spectacle, and in small intimacies (the hospital sequences with the child Wendy in MGN #1 show preserved hedonic capacity hours from death).

### 4.3.2 Persistent Depressive Disorder (Dysthymia) — Ruled Out

The required two-year (Terran-calibrated) continuous low mood is not met. Affect is event-congruent throughout; periods of buoyancy (early Starlin cosmic awakening, post-Thanos-defeat sequences) are clearly documented.

### 4.3.3 Adjustment Disorder with Mixed Anxious/Depressive Features — Present, Time-Limited, Adaptive

MGN #1 documents an unambiguous adjustment reaction to the cancer diagnosis: brief denial, displaced anger (notably at Mentor and the Rigellians), short dysphoric episode, then movement to acceptance. Duration is compressed — what Kübler-Ross frames as months-to-years collapses into days-to-weeks for him. This is *not* pathology; it is an adaptive reaction handled with unusual cognitive bandwidth and a pre-existing meaning-framework. Resolves within the diagnostic window. **Code as adjustment disorder, resolved, with note that resolution speed reflects pre-trauma rehearsal of mortality via Cosmic Awareness, not denial or dissociation.**

### 4.3.4 Bipolar Spectrum — Ruled Out

No manic, hypomanic, or mixed episodes. Energy expenditures during cosmic operations are sustained, task-locked, and followed by appropriate down-regulation, not by elevated mood or grandiose ideation. Cosmic Awareness might superficially mimic the expanded perceptual frame of mania, but the content is empirically validated (it works), accompanied by no pressured speech, no decreased need for sleep beyond Kree baseline, and no impulsivity.

### 4.3.5 Prolonged Grief Disorder — Considered, Sub-Threshold

Following Una's death he sustains grief but does not meet the persistence-and-impairment threshold (DSM-5-TR PGD requires 12+ months of disabling yearning/preoccupation). His grief is *converted* — into mission, into mentorship of women he will not allow himself to romance the way he romanced her (Carol Danvers is the clearest instance) — but is not disabling. Some clinicians might argue this conversion *is* avoidance in mature dress; the counter-evidence is his capacity to speak directly of Una when asked, without dysregulation.

---

## 4.4 Anxiety and Obsessive-Compulsive Spectrum

### 4.4.1 Generalized Anxiety / Panic — Ruled Out

No documented panic episodes. Worry behavior, where present, is task-tethered (operational planning, concern for Rick Jones's survival) rather than free-floating. Autonomic signatures of pathological anxiety (tremor, sweating, derealization) absent across observed combat and non-combat contexts.

### 4.4.2 Obsessive-Compulsive Personality Features — Present, Sub-Clinical

Meets several OCPD trait criteria: conscientiousness to a high degree, duty-orientation, emotional restriction in interpersonal contexts, perfectionism in mission execution, reluctance to delegate matters he considers his ethical responsibility. *Does not* meet disorder threshold because: (a) cognitive and behavioral flexibility are preserved (he revises priors against Kree indoctrination, accepts the Eon reframing, modifies tactics fluidly); (b) warmth in close relationships is preserved; (c) he *does* delegate (Rick handles Earth-life when Mar-Vell is in the Negative Zone, and Mar-Vell does not micromanage); (d) no hoarding, no miserliness, no rigid moralism imposed on others. **Best captured as OCPD-spectrum traits, sub-clinical, ego-syntonic, functionally adaptive within his operational role.**

### 4.4.3 Obsessive-Compulsive Disorder (proper) — Ruled Out

No intrusive obsessions, no compulsive rituals, no contamination or symmetry concerns. His asceticism is values-driven, not compulsion-driven.

---

## 4.5 Personality-Disorder Differential

A rigorous rule-out is necessary because Mar-Vell's surface presentation — restraint, withdrawal, self-sacrifice, role-fusion — could be misread by an unsophisticated observer.

### 4.5.1 Schizoid Personality Disorder — Ruled Out

Surface match: solitary cosmic vigils, asceticism, emotional restriction, indifference to social reward. Disqualifying counter-evidence: he forms *deep* emotional bonds (Una, Rick, Carol, Eros, Mentor); he experiences and expresses warmth, tenderness, and grief; his social withdrawal is contextual (cosmic duty, terminal illness, Negative Zone exile) not characterological; he derives meaning from relational care. Schizoid pathology requires *anhedonia for relationship*; he has the opposite — he is moved by relationship and disciplined in expression.

### 4.5.2 Schizotypal — Ruled Out

Cosmic Awareness produces phenomena that could superficially resemble magical thinking or unusual perceptual experiences, but the percepts are veridical (other cosmic-aware entities confirm them) and his cognition is otherwise hyper-organized.

### 4.5.3 Avoidant Personality Disorder — Ruled Out

He does not avoid difficult interpersonal material. He confronts Yon-Rogg, the Supreme Intelligence, Thanos, and his own death directly. The interpersonal distancing pattern noted in 4.2.2 is a trauma-related conversion of intimacy into duty, *not* a fear-of-rejection avoidance. He is not rejection-sensitive; he is intimacy-cautious in a specific, post-traumatic, partner-loss-related way.

### 4.5.4 Narcissistic Personality Disorder — Ruled Out, Emphatically

Given cosmic powers, public veneration on multiple worlds, and a literal title of "Protector of the Universe," the absence of narcissistic inflation is diagnostic in itself. No grandiosity, no entitlement (he accepts the Eon mandate with explicit humility, asks what it requires of him rather than what it grants him), no exploitation of subordinates, no envy of peers, no fragile self-esteem requiring mirroring. He treats Rick — a teenager with no powers when their bond begins — as a moral equal. This is anti-narcissistic structure.

### 4.5.5 Borderline — Ruled Out

Stable self-concept, stable interpersonal patterns, no impulsivity, no self-harm, no abandonment panic, no affective lability. The opposite profile.

### 4.5.6 Antisocial — Ruled Out

Conscience hypertrophied rather than absent. Strict adherence to internally held ethical code even at total personal cost.

### 4.5.7 Dependent — Ruled Out

Self-reliant to the point of pathological privatization of suffering (see 4.5.9), the opposite of dependent.

### 4.5.8 Histrionic — Ruled Out

Under-expressive rather than over-expressive; no attention-seeking, no theatrical affect.

### 4.5.9 The One Real Personality-Level Concern: *Privatization of Suffering*

If a personality-level pathology must be named at all, it is a sub-clinical pattern of refusal-to-be-cared-for. He will not request help; will not disclose pain until forced; will not permit himself to be a recipient of the care he routinely provides. This sits at the intersection of OCPD-style self-reliance, dismissing-attachment residue, and a soldier's ethic of not burdening subordinates. It is *not* a disorder, but it is a *vulnerability*, and it nearly cost him the only humane dying available to him — MGN #1 shows him learning, in the final weeks, to *receive* presence (Rick, Carol, Mentor, Drax, even Thanos in spectral aspect). The dying is partly the un-learning of this pattern, which suggests he himself recognized it as a flaw to be corrected before completion.

### 4.5.10 Martyr Complex / Pathological Self-Sacrifice — Ruled Out

He does not seek suffering, does not perform sacrifice for witness, does not refuse rescue when the calculus favors it. In MGN #1 he refuses *low-probability* interventions on rational grounds and explicitly states he wants to die well, not to die. The distinction matters: a martyr wants the death-as-statement; he wants the *completion-as-integrity*.

---

## 4.6 Substance Use and Behavioral Addictions

Negative across the canon. No alcohol use depicted (a Kree military soldier's discipline appears to extend here), no analgesic dependence even in terminal illness when offered Rigellian palliatives, no behavioral addictions (no compulsive combat-seeking, no compulsive sexual behavior, no compulsive work-as-flight). The absence of self-medicating behavior under his trauma load is itself remarkable and consistent with the mature-defense profile.

---

## 4.7 Cognitive and Neurocognitive Status

No documented cognitive decline. Cognitive flexibility, working memory, executive function, and meta-cognitive insight are preserved through terminal illness — cancer of the type depicted would, in a Terran, often produce cognitive sequelae from cachexia, paraneoplastic effects, or CNS involvement; Kree physiology and Nega-Band suppression apparently buffer this until very late. The hallucinatory Thanos sequence in MGN #1 is best read not as delirium but as a *constructed psychopompic dialogue* under Cosmic Awareness — phenomenologically vivid, internally coherent, and accepted by him as symbolic rather than literal.

---

## 4.8 Risk Assessment (retrospective, longitudinal)

- **Suicide risk:** Persistently low. He values life, including his own, throughout. The acceptance of death in MGN #1 is not suicidality; he accepts an external disease process rather than ending himself, and he resists premature endings.
- **Risk to others (non-combatant):** Persistently negligible. Robust impulse control; no displaced aggression; civilians treated with care even in operational chaos.
- **Risk to self via under-self-care:** *Moderate to high, chronically.* Privatization of suffering meant the cancer was likely symptomatic earlier than acknowledged and that the Nega-Bands' suppression masked what timely disclosure might have addressed. His one durable risk pattern is *not telling anyone he is hurt*.
- **Risk of moral injury sequelae:** Moderate, well-compensated. The Yon-Rogg betrayal, the killing he did in service of a cause he came to reject, and the deaths of those he failed to save (cumulative across cosmic-scale battles) constitute a substantial moral-injury load. He metabolized it via the Protector reframing rather than via avoidance or numbing.

---

## 4.9 Course Over Time

- **Phase I — Operational Kree Officer (pre-Earth through *MSH* #12, early *CM* vol. 1):** Acute stress reactivity within professional range. Sub-clinical hypervigilance. Sublimation defenses already operational.
- **Phase II — Exile and Bereavement (post-#11):** Acute grief reaction, time-limited; no progression to PGD. Identity destabilization brief; reconstituted around protective duty toward Earth.
- **Phase III — Forced Symbiosis (post-#17):** Adjustment reaction to loss of bodily sovereignty. No dissociative pathology despite the unprecedented somatic intrusion. Develops working alliance with Rick.
- **Phase IV — Cosmic Awakening (Starlin, #25–34):** *Resolution phase.* External meaning-frame installed by Eon stabilizes prior trauma load. Post-traumatic growth markers visible: deepened spirituality, revised priorities, strengthened sense of personal agency within larger purpose, enhanced relational appreciation (even as he expresses it through duty).
- **Phase V — Ascetic Guardianship (#35–62):** Steady state. Sub-clinical OCPD traits and privatization-of-suffering pattern most visible here. Mild relational impoverishment relative to capacity. Otherwise stable.
- **Phase VI — Terminal (MGN #1):** Adjustment reaction → integration → completion. Un-learning of the privatization pattern. Receives care. Dies cognitively intact, affectively appropriate, relationally reconciled.

The longitudinal shape is *not* a decompensation curve. It is a curve of progressive integration, with the terminal phase functioning as a final consolidation rather than a collapse.

---

## 4.10 Comorbidity Map

The conventional comorbidities one would expect given his etiological load — PTSD + MDD, PTSD + SUD, C-PTSD + BPD features, chronic pain + opioid dependence in terminal phase — are *all absent*. The only meaningful co-presentation is:

- **Sub-syndromal trauma-related interpersonal distancing** *with*
- **Sub-clinical OCPD traits** *with*
- **Time-limited adjustment reaction (terminal phase)** *with*
- **Privatization-of-suffering pattern (personality-level vulnerability, not disorder).**

These cluster coherently. They describe a high-functioning, mature-defense personality with one durable post-traumatic relational footprint and one durable self-care vulnerability. Nothing in the cluster is disabling; the cluster is, in fact, *protective* against the more severe presentations that the etiology would predict.

---

## 4.11 Summary Diagnostic Formulation

**Provisional formulation (cross-walked DSM-5-TR / ICD-11):**

- *Other Specified Trauma- and Stressor-Related Disorder* (DSM-5-TR 309.89 analog) / *Other specified disorders specifically associated with stress* (ICD-11 6B4Y), with the specifier *sub-syndromal, with mature defensive integration and post-traumatic growth features*.
- *Adjustment Disorder with Mixed Anxious/Depressed Mood* (DSM-5-TR 309.28), terminal phase only, *resolved*.
- *Obsessive-Compulsive Personality traits*, sub-clinical, ego-syntonic, *not rising to disorder*.
- *Personality-level vulnerability: privatization of suffering / refusal-to-receive-care* — descriptive, not a coded diagnosis.

**Etiological summary:** A constitutionally resilient individual subjected to severe but discrete and meaning-able traumatic insults within an emotionally restrictive military culture, who developed mature defenses early, received an externally validated transcendent meaning-frame at the critical post-trauma juncture (Eon, *CM* #29), and consolidated growth rather than pathology. The clinical picture sits in the post-traumatic growth literature rather than in any disorder category.

**Prognostic note (terminal, retrospective):** The dying was the best-organized, most cognitively intact, most relationally reconciled completion this analyst has on file across the cosmic-tier subject set. The behaviors that nearly compromised it — privatization of suffering, delayed disclosure — were corrected by the subject himself in the final weeks. This is not a person whose disorders killed him. This is a person whose discipline allowed him to die.

*End Section 4. Proceed to Section 5: Personality.*


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: MAR-VELL OF THE KREE

*Section 5 of dossier. Cross-reference §3 (Psychological) and §4 (Psychiatric) for etiology. This atlas catalogs the granular, observable behaviors — postural, verbal, gestural, decisional, ritualistic — by condition. Where a single tell appears across multiple conditions, the differential is noted. All behaviors derived from canonical record (Lee/Colan founding, Thomas, Englehart, Wein, Moench, Starlin terminal arc, posthumous fragments) and the established somatic-psychological profile.*

---

## I. BASELINE — RESTING STATE / OFF-DUTY CALM

The subject is rarely observed in true calm; "calm" for Mar-Vell is a low-grade operational standby, not a civilian relaxation. The distinction matters: a hostile analyst will mistake his quiet for repose and underestimate his readiness.

**Posture and somatics.** Standing: weight slightly forward on the balls of the feet, shoulders dropped but not collapsed, hands loose at the sides or clasped lightly behind the back in the parade-rest residue of Kree militia training. Seated: upright, never slumped, both feet planted; he does not cross his legs in mixed company (a Kree convention retained without comment). When he sits in human furniture he leaves the lower-back unsupported by the chair-back — a posture maintained for decades whose origin is military but whose persistence is identitarian.

**Breath.** Slow and diaphragmatic. Resting respiration is metronomic and unusually deep; observed witnesses (Rick Jones internally; Carol Danvers obliquely) register it as "too quiet." The Nega-Band-era physiology permits long voluntary apneas; in standby he uses this unconsciously, holding the bottom of an exhale a half-beat longer than human norm.

**Gaze.** Soft middle-distance default, with periodic, almost ritual sweeps of the room — entrances, exits, ceiling, hands of every present party. The sweep is fast (under two seconds) and so habitual it reads as inattention. He locks eyes when addressed, holds the lock through the entire utterance, breaks it deliberately when finished. He does not glance away to think; he closes his eyes briefly instead.

**Speech.** Low register, measured cadence, sentences fully constructed before delivery. Minimal filler. He uses the second-person "you" sparingly and the first-person "I" only when responsibility must be unambiguously claimed. Prefers infinitive and conditional constructions ("To act now would be…") — a syntactic residue of translation from Kree, retained because it preserves analytic distance.

**Idle behaviors.** When unobserved he reads — Earth texts in his middle period (history, ethics, astronomy), Kree military histories rarely. He keeps the Nega-Bands inert against the skin and occasionally turns them on the wrist, a quarter-rotation at a time, the way a man with a wedding ring will turn it without noticing. This is the closest thing to a self-soothing tic he possesses.

**Eating and drinking.** Abstemious. Eats once per cycle when alone, twice when in company (a courtesy). No alcohol, no Kree intoxicants, no stimulants. Drinks water at room temperature. Eats slowly, sets utensils down between bites, finishes everything served. Refuses second portions politely; never explains why.

**Sleep.** Short by human standards — four to five hours, monophasic, lights off, no ambient sound. Wakes at a self-set time without external prompt. Does not linger in bed.

---

## II. OPERATIONAL CALM — DUTY ACTIVE, NO ACTIVE THREAT

The shift from baseline to operational is subtle and a key diagnostic. Observers who know him well (Rick, Carol, eventually Mentor) detect it; strangers do not.

**Posture.** Weight redistributes to a true neutral stance: equal pressure on both feet, knees micro-bent, hands free. Shoulders rise approximately one centimeter.

**Gaze.** The room-sweep cadence shortens from ~90-second intervals to ~30-second intervals. He begins to track personnel by silhouette rather than face. He will identify the load-bearing structural elements of any new environment within his first minute inside it; this is not conscious but it is reliable.

**Speech.** Shortens. Drops conditional constructions for declaratives. Begins to issue what would be commands if he held command authority; in their absence they emerge as suggestions phrased as observations ("The eastern approach is unguarded"). Tone drops further; volume does not rise.

**Nega-Band ritual.** Before any operation of expected duration, he brings the Bands together at the wrist — not the transformative clap, but a brief contact, palms aligned, eyes closed for one to two seconds. This is invariant across the canon. It functions as both a systems-check and a small private liturgy. He does this even when alone, even when he believes himself unobserved.

**Eating before operations.** Refuses food in the four hours preceding planned engagement. Drinks water only. He will eat afterward, methodically, regardless of outcome.

---

## III. ACUTE THREAT / COMBAT ONSET

The most observed and documented condition. The behavioral signature is *de-escalation of affect concurrent with escalation of capability* — the opposite of the standard combatant profile.

**Pre-engagement (seconds to minutes before contact).** Breath deepens further and slows. Heart rate (per Kree physiology and Nega-Band telemetry) drops rather than rises. He becomes slightly *quieter* in body — fewer micro-movements, no fidget. The room-sweep becomes continuous and ceases to be visible; he is now reading the entire field without turning his head, an artifact of Cosmic Awareness in late period and trained peripheral vigilance throughout.

**Verbal output.** Drops to near zero. He gives warnings — almost always to the opponent, almost always once, almost always specific ("Stand down. I will not ask again."). He does not banter. He does not threaten. He names what he will do if compliance fails, and then he does exactly that. The literalism is a tell: an adversary who has fought him before will know that the warning is the entire negotiation.

**Engagement.** Movement is economical. He does not telegraph; the body is square to the opponent at the moment of strike, never wound up. He prefers single decisive contact to extended exchange — a knockout opening, not a brawl. When the Nega-Bands fire, he fires *through* a target rather than at it, a doctrinal habit. He does not pursue downed opponents. He does not strike a second time when the first has sufficed.

**Tactical decision habits under threat.**
- Civilians located first, isolated from the combat envelope before opponent is engaged.
- Structural collapse risk assessed before high-yield discharge.
- Lethal force reserved for credible existential threat; he prefers incapacitation, accepts the additional risk this imposes on himself.
- Opponent's communication channels (literal or relational) preserved where possible — he keeps the door to surrender open longer than any of his peers.
- When outmatched, he buys time rather than spending lives; he will absorb damage personally to delay an opponent's reach to others.

**Affective tells under threat.** A faint tightening at the jaw on the left side, observable in close-quarters panels across the Thomas and Starlin runs. The mouth does not set into a hard line; it relaxes. Anger, when it arrives, manifests as *slowed* speech, not raised. The eyes do not narrow; they widen slightly. He has been seen to smile in combat exactly twice in the canonical record, both in the late period, both in moments of recognizing an opponent's competence — a tell unfortunate enough to read as serenity in a man about to kill you.

**The Yon-Rogg exception.** With Yon-Rogg specifically, all of the above modulations destabilize. Combat with Yon-Rogg shows faster breath, increased verbalization (accusations, named grievances), greater willingness to extend the exchange beyond decisive resolution. This is the only opponent in the file against whom he behaves like an ordinary man. After Una's death, the destabilization deepens but never produces lethal escalation; he stops short, every time, and reports the discipline of stopping as costlier than the discipline of striking would have been.

---

## IV. CHRONIC STRESS / EXTENDED ADVERSITY

Distinguished from acute threat by duration; the behavioral picture is degenerative-disciplinary rather than reactive.

**Withdrawal.** Increased solo time. Refuses social meals. Defers to Rick Jones for "normal life" intervals in the symbiotic period, then returns to the Negative Zone for what reads as recovery but functions as voluntary isolation.

**Asceticism intensifies.** Food intake decreases further. Sleep duration shortens (a counterintuitive response — most stressed beings sleep more or worse; he sleeps less and well). Reading shifts toward ethics and cosmology, away from history.

**Verbal restraint increases.** He becomes harder to draw into conversation. When pressed, he gives accurate but minimal accounts of his interior state. He does not lie about being unwell; he simply declines to elaborate.

**Drill behaviors.** Repetition of Kree militia katas in private — observed by Rick Jones across the symbiosis as flashes in the shared mind. The drills are technically obsolete; he runs them for the somatic structure, not the combat utility. A surveillance asset would note that the drill sequence is identical from his first canonical depiction to his last; it has not been updated.

**Decisional habits under chronic stress.** Time horizons lengthen. He plans further out, commits more conservatively, refuses optional engagements, declines invitations to peripheral conflicts. He becomes harder to recruit, easier to rely on for what he has already committed to. He does not abandon obligations under stress; he *narrows* them.

---

## V. INTIMACY — ROMANTIC AND DEEP RELATIONAL

A sparse but well-documented condition. The canonical evidence runs through three subjects: Una (early, full), Carol Danvers (middle, sublimated), Rick Jones (continuous, involuntary, eventually fraternal).

**Approach behaviors.** He does not initiate physical intimacy; he receives it when offered and reciprocates fully. He does initiate emotional intimacy via shared task — teaching, training, planning. Vulnerability is delivered in fragments, usually obliquely, often through what he reveals about cosmology or duty rather than about himself directly. A confession with Mar-Vell will sound like a lecture; the personal content is in the choice of subject, not the disclosure.

**Touch.** Sparing, deliberate, terminal-weight — when he touches a loved one, the contact is firm, brief, and complete; he does not maintain contact passively. Hands to shoulders more than to faces.
